***патефон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:патефон.html>патефо́н</a> (11956)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">Pathéphone</i> (trade mark) for a phonograph made by the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Path%C3%A9" class="extiw" title="w:Pathé">Pathé Brothers Company</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:патефон.html>патефо́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">patefón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:патефон.html>патефо́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:патефон.html>патефо́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:патефон.html>патефо́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> portable gramophone, phonograph</li></ol>

***патологический.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:патологический.html>патологи́ческий</a> (7537)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:патология.html>патоло́гия</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">patológija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:патологический.html>патологи́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">patologíčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>pathological <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">various senses</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***патрон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:патрон.html>патро́н</a> (2589)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Patrone</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:патрон.html>патро́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">patrón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:патрон.html>патро́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:патрон.html>патро́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:патрон.html>патро́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cartridge, shell, <i>plural</i> ammunition
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боевой.html>боево́й</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:патрон.html>патро́н</a></strong></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bojevój patrón</i> ― <span class="e-translation">live cartridge</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">подносчик <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:патрон.html>патро́нов</a></strong></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podnosčik patrónov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ammunition carrier</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:холостой.html>холосто́й</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:патрон.html>патро́н</a></strong></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xolostój patrón</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blank cartridge</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учебный.html>уче́бный</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:патрон.html>патро́н</a></strong></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">učébnyj patrón</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dummy cartridge</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mechanical engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chuck</li>
<li>lamp socket</li>
<li>tailor's pattern</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:патронташ.html>патронта́ш</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">patrontáš</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***пахарь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пахарь.html>па́харь</a> (19147)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пахать.html>паха́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paxátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to plow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-арь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-arʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пахарь.html>па́харь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">páxarʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пахарь.html>па́харя</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пахарь.html>па́хари</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пахарь.html>па́харей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>plowman</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> farmer</li></ol>

***пахать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пахать.html>паха́ть</a> (7812)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pāxàti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пахать.html>паха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">paxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to plow</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to work hard</li></ol>

***пахнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пахнуть.html>пахну́ть</a> (999)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*paxnǫti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пахнуть.html>па́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">páxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to smell (of), to savour
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пахнуть.html>па́хнут</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dénʹgi ne <b>páxnut</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Money has no smell.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to smell, to reek (of) (+ instrumental case)</li></ol>

<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">

<ul><li>(no equivalent)</li>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пропа́хивать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">propáxivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

</p>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запахнуть.html>запа́хнуть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zapáxnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li>(no equivalent)</li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пропахнуть.html>пропа́хнуть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">propáxnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*paxnǫti</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:паче.html>па́че</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pače</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">more</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, comparative of <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">пакы</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paky</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">again, moreover</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*paky</i>. ***пачка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пачка.html>пачка</a> (1970)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пак</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and the former from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Pack</i>. See also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паковать.html>пакова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pakovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пачка.html>па́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">páčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пачка.html>па́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пачка.html>па́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пачка.html>па́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bundle, pack, packet, batch, sheaf, package, parcel</li>
<li>tutu</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clip (ammunition)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***пачкать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пачкать.html>па́чкать</a> (17615)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">paćkać</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">ciapka</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пачкать.html>па́чкать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">páčkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испачкать.html>испа́чкать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запачкать.html>запа́чкать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to soil, to dirty, to stain</li>
<li>to daub</li></ol>

***пашня.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пашня.html>па́шня</a> (16331)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пахать.html>паха́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paxátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пашня.html>па́шня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pášnja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пашня.html>па́шни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пашня.html>па́шни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пашня.html>па́шен</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ploughed field, arable land</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пахать.html>паха́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">paxátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вспахать.html>вспаха́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vspaxátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
